Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageGood Samaritan Society contact form
URLhttps://www.good-sam.com/contact-us
Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score1016
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1016, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 145. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 16. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 160

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 123 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 42 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 45 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue contrastAAA

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 109

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r66, score 91 (Text contrast less than AAA requires)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 15 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 18 (Text has insufficient contrast)
  • Package tenon, test 95, score 8 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 68

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 46 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 20 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 30 (Very low contrast)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 55

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 53 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 26

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 24 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Issue targetSize

WCAG: 2.5.5

Score: 23

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 152, score 21 (Actionable element is smaller than the minimum required size)

Issue contrastRisk

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 21

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_3_F24.F24.FGColour, score 1 (Inline foreground color may lack a complementary background color)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Abs, score 1 (Contrast between the absolutely positioned text and its background may be less than 7:1)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G17.BgImage, score 16 (Contrast between the text and its background image may be less than 7:1)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Abs, score 1 (Contrast between the absolutely positioned text and its background may be less than 4.5:1)
